2013-09-01 00:13:00,749 [12376] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode
2013-09-01 00:13:04,684 [12376] DEBUG Sys - 
select 1
from sys_roleMenuMap A
left join sys_userRoleMap B on B.RoleCode = A.RoleCode
left join sys_menu C on C.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.UserCode = 'lhs'
and C.URL in ('/Sys/generator/Index','/Sys/generator')
2013-09-01 00:13:08,948 [13356] DEBUG Mms - SELECT Name as TableName FROM sys.tables order by Name
2013-09-01 00:13:10,028 [9836] DEBUG Mms - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_dealDetail')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

FROM sys.columns

from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2013-09-01 01:20:46,407 [12008] DEBUG Mms - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_deal')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_deal')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2013-09-01 08:35:08,565 [8616] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

FROM sys.columns

		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_material')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_dealDetail')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2013-09-01 08:57:28,189 [16164] DEBUG Mms - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_checkDetail')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_material')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2013-09-01 10:36:54,381 [9488] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_directDetail')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2013-09-01 12:30:06,033 [7356] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode
2013-09-01 12:30:16,981 [7356] DEBUG Sys - 
select 1
from sys_roleMenuMap A
left join sys_userRoleMap B on B.RoleCode = A.RoleCode
left join sys_menu C on C.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.UserCode = 'lhs'
and C.URL in ('/Sys/generator/Index','/Sys/generator')

		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_checkDetail')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_buildPart')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('sys_codeType')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2013-09-01 15:36:50,827 [14104] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode
2013-09-01 15:36:51,395 [11836] DEBUG Sys -

from sys_roleMenuMap A
left join sys_userRoleMap B on B.RoleCode = A.RoleCode
left join sys_menu C on C.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.UserCode = 'lhs'
and C.URL in ('/Sys/generator/Index','/Sys/generator')

2013-09-01 15:37:15,623 [11836] DEBUG Mms - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_deal')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_directDetail')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_directDetail')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_directDetail')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2013-09-01 21:53:11,284 [9464] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('sys_codeType')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2013-09-01 23:11:59,660 [9568] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'lhs' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'lhs'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_deal')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'

  )  
)

						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('mms_deal')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id
